<review>My wife and I first attended The Rock Church Temecula Valley in August 2012. On this particular Sunday the Senior Pastor Hennie was out on a mission trip in South Africa. His lovely wife Pastor Miranda preached part 2 of a series titled: "Can You Hear Me Now". We both left with with an immense sense of fulfillment. <userid>104391725146946372378</userid>< name>
Julie Healon< /name>
<Date>1515384039035<//Date>< rating>
5</rating>
< text>
Yum! Been years since I've been here. The tables are sticky, the floors are filthy, but the food is plentiful and delicious. A little pricey. But delicious.  Lots and lots of seating. It wasn't busy on a Sunday, about noon.

I ordered the number 29. It came with beef and teriyaki chicken. Maybe bbq? Not sure. I absolutely LOVED the beef. Delicious! So much flavor. The chicken was pretty good. Juicy. It came with white rice and veggies. The veggies are on the hard side. Steamed, So they are warm. Very crunchy. Broccoli, carrot, and zucchini.

My hubby got the number 84. It was a salad, with dressing. Not sure what the dressing was, but he loved it. It also had the teriyaki chicken, like I had. Good. And a couple pieces of breaded chicken with sauce. That was really good! Some macaroni salad, that was pretty good. And some tempura. A shrimp, a broccoli, a piece of squash, and a carrot. All were really good.

We shared some egg rolls. They don't have sweet and sour sauce, but the sauce they give you with them is really good. And sweet. I also got a mango boba smoothie. That was AMAZING. I want one every day! It tasted like a starburst. So so good! And hubby got a sprite.

For all our food, it was about 30 bucks. Such good food. Yummy! Will definitely be back.< /text>

An innovative restaurant turning you into a tepanyaki chef! The attendants are very nice and helpful. <user_name>Gary Chow< /user_name>< Text>
Similar to Pepper Lunch. We arrived around 12:30 on a Sunday and the place was full.  Wood (fake?) and stainless vibe; typical of this type of restaurant. The staff seats you and you order via table service.  Overall impressed with the staff's courtesy and professionalism.  We ordered the kimchi beef rice and the garlic beef rice.  They also have takoyaki, fries, calamari and other sides.  Portion and flavor are good though the price is on the upper end. Afterwards I feel a bit lightheaded, so maybe there's msg in the garlic soy sauce?  Nevertheless, it's worth a second try; will try the sides and the curry next time.< /Text>

<date>1527996083945< /date></record>

< Text>
I was not aware of Family Dollar until I saw an ad in my local circular.  Oddly though, there are no Family Dollars within 5 miles of my residence.  The store's website locator indicated that this locations was my closest.  Armed with coupons I drove the 7.85 miles on a rainy LA afternoon in search of some deals.

As I entered the lot, there were plenty of parking spot, I thought perhaps an indicator that the deals inside were not that great.  The store itself is pretty small; on average smaller than your 99 cent only and Dollar Tree store.

However, what sets Family Dollar aside from the aforementioned discount outlets is that Family Dollar carries bigger ticket items that you would find at Target at even deeper discounts.

For example, I was able to get Tide Pods (14 count) for $2.50 with coupon and Downy Infusion (32 oz) for $1.95 with coupon - both exceptional deals.  I ended up stocking up on my household items.  My total at the register for my monthly household items was $78.67 - which at Target would have cost me nearly double this.  But the best part was that after manufacturer coupons and an in-store $5.00 off coupon my total was $38.80!!< /Text>
